From animals and flowers to scenes of people working on the farm and children playing, the paintings mirrored the unique charm and beauty of the lifestyle in the town and surrounding countryside.;从动物和花卉到人们在农场工作和孩子们玩耍的场景，这些画反映了城镇和周边乡村生活方式的独特魅力和美丽。

From 2019 to May 2022, Yuan wrote 30 articles trying to answer these questions from scientific perspectives, which have been published recently as a book, Jiaoshou Yu Nianqingren,.;2019年至2022年5月，袁征撰写了30篇文章，试图从科学的角度回答这些问题，最近以一本书的形式出版了《交手于念情人》。
From 2019 to May 2022, Yuan wrote 30 articles trying to answer these questions from scientific perspectives, which have been published recently as a book, Jiaoshou Yu Nianqingren, by Citic Press.;2019年至2022年5月，袁征撰写了30篇文章，试图从科学的角度回答这些问题，最近由中信出版社出版了《交手于念情人》一书。
